### 27. 奢华社论肖像：成熟女性提示

### 49. 高级时装电影感人像摄影：快门拖影效果

**Author**: [FL⭕RA](https://x.com/Flora_Janer8)  **Date**: 2026-02-04  **Language**: en

> 生成一张戏剧性、时尚感十足的电影肖像，描绘一位身穿黑色天鹅绒礼服的女性（形似萨迪·辛克）。关键特征是使用单色深红色影棚灯光，并采用“慢门拖影”或长曝光效果，在人物面部后方营造出空灵的运动模糊拖影。

![高级时装电影感人像摄影：快门拖影效果](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770273435289_xg6dtq_HAUc8wpWUAE_oiU.jpg)

```
"A high-fashion cinematic portrait of a woman with wavy auburn hair, wearing a deep-V neck black velvet gown. The scene is drenched in a monochromatic {argument name="lighting color" default="deep red"} studio light. A 'shutter drag' or long-exposure effect creates a ghostly, ethereal motion blur trailing to the right of her face. She has a poised, high-glance expression with bold red lipstick. One hand is gracefully touching her neck, showing a statement ring. Moody, dramatic shadows, 8k resolution, shot on 35mm lens, fashion editorial style."
>
Breakdown of Details
| Element | Description |
|---|---|
| Lighting | Saturated red monochromatic lighting with high contrast (Chiaroscuro effect). |
| Technical Effect | Shutter Drag / Motion Blur: The "ghosting" effect behind the head suggests movement during a slow exposure. |
| Subject | A woman with fair skin, freckles, and wavy {argument name="hair color" default="ginger/auburn"} hair. |
| Wardrobe | A minimalist, elegant black dress with a plunging neckline that contrasts sharply against the red background. |
| Composition | Medium shot, centered, with a soft-focus vignette that draws attention to the face and hands. |
Tips for Customizing
 * To change the mood: Replace "deep red" with "electric blue" or "neon emerald" for a different vibe.
 * To change the model: You can specify "shorter hair," "different ethnicity," or "alternative clothing" while keeping the "motion blur" and "monochromatic light" tags to maintain the style.
```

[[Motion Blur Effect]] [[Cinematic Fashion]] [[Long Exposure Photography]]

### 67. 建筑平面图与逼真室内照片生成

**Author**: [摆烂程序媛](https://x.com/wanerfu)  **Date**: 2026-02-04  **Language**: zh

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示，旨在生成一张分割构图图像：左侧展示一张详细、极简主义的建筑平面图插画，右侧展示一张对应客厅的超现实室内照片，强调概念与现实之间的对比。它为两部分都指定了风格、光照、调色板和技术细节。

![建筑平面图与逼真室内照片生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770273487845_ffq4i6_HAS7qE7bsAAE3VO.jpg)

```
分割构图，左右两半清晰划分。

左半部分：
现代极简风格的详细建筑平面图插画，与参考相匹配。俯视图住宅布局，标注客厅、餐厅、开放式厨房、卧室、门厅、阳台、凸窗和流线。米色和暖灰色调，清晰线条，柔和阴影，微妙纹理，室内设计演示风格。专业建筑可视化，平面蓝图美学，家具布局清晰。

右半部分：
平面图所示客厅的超逼真室内摄影。客厅家具齐全，空间布局精确对应平面图：{argument name="家具组合" default="弧形沙发组合、中央茶几、柔和地毯、温暖木地板、中性墙面、大窗户自然采光"}。现代、舒适、当代室内设计，土色调，柔和光线，逼真材质和生活细节。

右半应如真实室内照片，左半保持清晰建筑图纸。两部分视觉对齐，清晰展示'概念对比现实'。

风格与氛围

建筑可视化遇见真实室内摄影
现代、温暖、优雅住宅设计
简洁、专业、设计工作室呈现
从概念到实现的对比

光影与色彩

左：平均光照、中性色调
右：自然日光、柔和阴影、温暖高光
平面图与房间色彩和谐统一

镜头与技术细节

左：俯视正交视图
右：室内广角镜头、眼平视角
高分辨率、细节清晰、逼真纹理

反向提示：
卡通风格、低细节、杂乱室内、布局不符、不现实比例、生硬光线、夸张色彩、文字叠加、水印
```

### 71. 低保真直闪抓拍人像（2000 年代初期美学）

**Author**: [Maercih](https://x.com/Maercihh)  **Date**: 2026-02-04  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于创作一张年轻女性的原始、纪录片风格肖像，旨在模仿 2000 年代初期数码快照的美学。它指定了“生活化”的环境、休闲的服装（超大乐队 T 恤）和刺眼的直射机内闪光灯，营造出平坦的照明、强烈的阴影和凉爽、柔和的调色板，并带有时间戳叠加。

![低保真直闪抓拍人像（2000 年代初期美学）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770273449213_tt68h9_HASuV4TagAAQk6P.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": "A candid, documentary-style indoor portrait of a young woman sitting on a worn fabric couch in a modest living room. She wears an oversized black graphic {argument name="clothing type" default="band T-shirt"} and loose black pants, styled casually with no visible effort. Her hair is loosely tied back, makeup minimal or absent, with natural skin texture and slight under-eye softness visible. She faces the camera directly with a calm, tired, introspective expression. The environment feels lived-in and slightly cluttered, with an old desktop computer, exposed cables, and dated furniture in the background. The image is captured using direct on-camera flash, creating flat, harsh lighting with strong shadows and a nostalgic early-digital-camera aesthetic. ### 84. 场景和姿态变化的混合工作流

**Author**: [浅野 美咲（Asano Misaki）](https://x.com/Asan0_Misaki)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 本文介绍了一种生成多样化图像的混合工作流程：首先，使用 Gemini 的 Nano Banana Pro (NBP) 创建基础图像，然后使用 Grok 平台改变场景和姿势。用户指出 NBP 在细节和 1K 质量方面表现出色，而 Grok 在场景变化方面速度更快。

      "dynamic_range": "natural_not_hdr",
      "skin_rendering": "real_texture_zero_retouch"
    },

    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "Photoreal winter portrait in heavy snowfall. Minimal snowy background with soft fog and low-contrast winter atmosphere. ### 104. 超逼真“Instagram 辣妹”风格的安娜·德·阿玛斯自拍

### 115. 电影级足球技巧和进球动画提示

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 AI 视频生成器 (Kling) 运动提示，描述了一个戏剧性的足球序列：一名球员以快速的脚步盘带过克里斯蒂亚诺·罗纳尔多，最终射门得分，伴随着电影般的镜头抖动、慢动作效果，并以交换球衣庆祝结束。

```
Motion prompt: The man begins dribbling the ball forward at speed. The camera switches to a slightly wider tracking shot, following his movement smoothly while introducing light horizontal camera shake from simulated shoulder-mounted broadcast footage.
Cristiano Ronaldo closes in aggressively to defend. As Ronaldo steps forward, the man performs rapid footwork—quick step-overs, a sudden body feint, and a sharp lateral cut.
At the exact moment he beats Ronaldo, the camera adds a short, intense impact shake to emphasize the skill move, followed by a fast push-in zoom.
The crowd volume spikes. Motion blur subtly increases on the legs and ball while the upper body stays sharp. The camera briefly shifts to a low-angle tracking shot, enhancing speed and dominance.
He accelerates toward the goal. As he strikes the ball, the camera performs a cinematic whip-pan, followed by a brief slow-motion beat at the moment of contact.
A strong vertical camera shake occurs as the ball rockets into the net, simulating crowd eruption and stadium vibration.
GOAL MOMENT (7s–8.5s):
The net ripples dramatically. Stadium lights flare slightly. Fans jump and wave scarves. The camera transitions into a subtle celebratory shake, as if the operator is reacting emotionally. Ronaldo turns back, smiling with admiration and respect.
END FRAME (8.5s–10s):
Transition smoothly into the provided final image.
Cristiano Ronaldo walks toward the man and hands him his Real Madrid jersey, clearly showing Ronaldo’s name and number 7 on the back. Both are smiling, breathing heavily, sharing a victorious moment. Camera stabilizes gradually, ending with a clean, steady cinematic frame under glowing stadium lights.
```

### 125. 爆炸图产品可视化提示

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的图像生成提示，要求生成上传产品的爆炸图，其中所有内部和外部组件都分离并悬浮在空中，按正确的组装顺序排列。它强调保留原始构图、光照和透视，以实现高端、技术性且超逼真的商业可视化效果。

```
IMAGE PROMPT - Create an exploded view of the uploaded product where all components are separated and floating in mid-air. Disassemble every visible part including internal structures, outer shell, mechanical elements, and small details, arranging them in correct assembly order with realistic spacing and proportions. Preserve the exact hand position (if present), grip, camera angle, framing, perspective, lighting, background, and overall composition from the original image. Only the product should separate into parts nothing else should change. Ensure parts are aligned along their natural axes, appearing as if frozen mid-assembly. Use photorealistic materials, sharp details, natural shadows, and accurate reflections so the result looks like a high-end commercial product visualization. Final image should feel modern, technical, ultra-realistic, and premium.
```

[[Technical Illustration]] [[Commercial Product Photography]]

### 126. 豪华休息室人像，配有霓虹氛围灯

**Author**: [Yaseen Khan Gul](https://x.com/YaseenK7212)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 一个 JSON 提示，用于生成一张逼真的时尚肖像照，描绘一位沙漏型身材的女性，身穿紧身米色紧身连衣裙，在夜晚的豪华休息室中斜倚在一面木墙上。该提示强调使用霓虹环境照明（蓝色、紫色、金色）和电影级调色，以突出拍摄对象的体态和奢华的环境。

![豪华休息室人像，配有霓虹氛围灯](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187158816_ulc2bc_HAO26clWAAAuKLX.jpg)

      "placement": "Cascading down her back"
    },

      "traits": [ "Full bust", "Tiny waist", "Wide hips", "Rounded prominent back" ]
    },
    "pose": {
      "position": "Side pose, leaning sideways against a wooden wall",
      "interaction": "Chest pressed firmly against the wall",
      "hand_placement": "One hand resting on hip"
    }
  },
  "attire": {
    "dress": {
      "type": "Bodycon midi dress",
      "color": "{argument name="dress color" default="Beige"}",
      "fit": "Tight-fitting, ruched stretch fabric clinging to figure",
      "features": [ "Sleeveless", "Thin spaghetti straps" ]
    },

Use the uploaded image of the character as an exact reference. Preserve the original proportions, materials, colors, textures, and facial features. Do not alter the design and do not stylize the character.

A first-person point-of-view shot inside an abandoned space [LOCATION TYPE: television studio/advertising set/real filming location].

The viewer is holding a flashlight, creating a single circular beam of light while the rest of the space is engulfed in darkness. In the flashlight beam, it is visible that the character is positioned as if it was left behind after filming: [POSITION: lying on the floor/curled up in a corner/leaning against a table/slumped against a wall]. The character must appear completely lifeless and inactive: no action, no intentional pose, no sense of presence. If it is a doll or a costume, there must be no visible hands, rods, strings, or person inside.

The character appears old, dirty, and abandoned: worn fabric, accumulated dust, stains, discoloration, flattened or damaged areas.

The environment is clearly abandoned: dusty surfaces, old filming equipment, cables scattered on the floor, faded signs or set decorations.

Dust particles float within the flashlight beam; the space feels silent and untouched for years.

Photorealistic flashlight-based lighting, harsh shadows, rough textures, documentary realism, on-location shooting aesthetics, no stylization Aspect

Ratio 9:16
```

日本人女性がオシャレな部屋でヨガをしているマルチカット。
画角を5×5で区切って、25個シーンを作成して。
各シーンの左上に通し番号を1から順に表示して。

上記画像には25個のシーンが描かれています。
左上がシーン番号です。
{argument name="抽出シーン番号" default="7"}番のシーンを抽出、高解像度で再現して。
```

### 150. Rosé (BLACKPINK) 磨砂玻璃海报提示词

**Author**: [Neonva](https://x.com/Neonva2623)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 这是一个复杂且分层的提示，用于创建一张 Rosé (BLACKPINK) 的逼真特写肖像海报。它需要两个叠加层：一个在强烈阳光下的清晰基础图像，以及一个全局应用的磨砂玻璃效果，但脸部中心通过一个单眼镜框形成一个“镜头窗口”除外，最终呈现出高对比度、现代图形海报的外观。

![Rosé (BLACKPINK) 磨砂玻璃海报提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187140602_zweuy3_HANteDQbMAAd9y3.jpg)

```
{
"subject": {
"description": "A realistic close-up portrait poster composed of two overlaid image layers. **Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

```
Motion Prompt: The pizza begins a slow, smooth rotation while its layers gently separate one by one, maintaining perfect alignment, spacing, and scale. Each ingredient floats apart with precise, controlled motion. The movement is clean and fluid, with no extra effects or distractions.

Start Frame: A high-quality, professional product photograph of a gourmet chicken pizza with a golden-brown crust, melted mozzarella cheese, and evenly distributed seasoned chicken pieces with tomato, onion and olives topping. The pizza looks hot, fresh, and appetizing with visible cheese stretch and baked texture. Minimalist style, shot against a pure solid white background with soft, natural shadows. Ultra-sharp focus, 8K resolution, clean and modern fast-food aesthetic.

End Frame: Create a hyper-realistic exploded vertical infographic composition of a chicken pizza.
At the top, a golden oven-baked pizza crust edge with light blistering and baked texture.
Below it, stretchy melted mozzarella cheese floating smoothly with natural cheese pull.
Under the cheese, juicy grilled or crispy chicken chunks with visible seasoning and moisture.
Next, fresh toppings such as sliced bell peppers, olives, and onions suspended mid-air.
Beneath the toppings, a rich tomato sauce layer with glossy depth.
At the bottom, a soft yet crisp pizza base, perfectly centered and aligned.
Pure solid white background, soft studio lighting, and subtle realistic shadows beneath each floating layer.
Ultra-sharp focus, DSLR macro photography look.
Clean, minimalist infographic text labels with thin pointer lines for each layer. Premium, professional, photorealistic food infographic style.

### 165. 咖啡机爆炸图产品可视化

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成 Scarlett 滴漏式咖啡机的超逼真 3D 爆炸图可视化，要求精确的垂直对齐、详细的组件标注以及特定的材质和灯光效果，以呈现高端广告的视觉效果。

```
Create a photorealistic premium exploded-view visualization of a Scarlett drip coffee maker, fully disassembled and aligned vertically along a central axis.

All components must levitate, remain evenly spaced, perfectly centered, and aligned with precise vertical symmetry.

COMPONENT LABELING (MANDATORY)
Each component must include: 

→ A thin white or light-gray arrow / leader line
→ A clean sans-serif label placed to the right side
→ Part name + short spec (minimal, technical text)
→ Labels must NOT overlap any object
→ Arrows must point clearly to the exact component

COMPONENTS (TOP → BOTTOM, ALL FLOATING & LABELED)

1 → Upper Lid
• Matte black plastic
• Minimal geometry
→ Label: Upper Lid ➝ Heat-Resistant Plastic

2 → Water Reservoir
• Semi-transparent plastic
• Visible water scale (1–6 cups)
→ Label: Water Reservoir — 0.6 L

3 → Water Delivery System
• Thin tubes + distributor
• Clean internal engineering
→ Label: Water Flow System — Even Distribution

4 → Heating Element (TEN)
• Metal body
• Subtle warm glow
→ Label: Heating Element — 600–800 W

5 → Filter Holder
• Black plastic
• Conical drip design
→ Label: Filter Holder — Drip System

6 → Reusable Mesh Filter
• Fine stainless-steel grid
→ Label: Reusable Filter — Stainless Steel

7 → Brewing Unit
• Visible internal channels
→ Label: Brewing Chamber — Coffee Extraction

8 → Glass Carafe
• Heat-resistant transparent glass
• Black handle
→ Label: Glass Carafe — Thermal Glass

9 → Warming Plate
• Metallic heating surface
→ Label: Warming Plate — Heat Retention

10 → Base Housing & Electronics
• Rubber feet
• Power button + cable
• Internal electronics
→ Label: Base Unit — Power & Control

VISUAL EFFECTS :

• Soft steam rising from brewing unit
• Gentle warm glow from heating element
• Soft shadows beneath each floating component
• Thin guide arrows indicating assembly order

BACKGROUND : 

• Dark premium gradient (graphite → deep gray)
• Very subtle concentric circles (heat & aroma concept)
• Clean, modern kitchen-tech aesthetic

LIGHTING : 

• Soft warm key light from top-left
• Rim lighting on glass & metal edges
• No harsh or dramatic shadows

CAMERA : 

• Front-facing
• Slight top-down tilt
• Vertical 9:16
• Product occupies ~70% of the frame

STYLE & QUALITY :-

• Ultra-realistic 3D render
• Premium household appliance advertising look
• Octane / Cinema 4D style
• PBR materials (plastic, glass, metal)
• 8K, ultra-sharp, portfolio-ready

NEGATIVE PROMPT
No logos
No watermark
No clutter

No cartoon or illustration style

![两罐汽水产品摄影提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100863541_qmzllv_HAMNF2yaYAAa48A.jpg)

```
IMAGE: Frame & Composition: The camera uses a low-angle, straight-on frontal view, positioned slightly below the subjects so the two cans rise above the horizon line; both cans are upright and vertically oriented, placed side by side with a narrow gap, occupying the central upper third of the frame; the lower edge crops into a metallic ledge that acts as a base plane, while the cans are fully visible from base to rim; the composition is symmetrical but slightly staggered in height, with the right can marginally taller in frame due to perspective; negative space dominates the upper background, reinforcing vertical emphasis and product isolation. Lighting & Atmosphere: A frontal key light, slightly elevated and centered, produces even illumination across both cans, generating dense, high-contrast specular highlights on condensation droplets; shadows are minimal and soft, indicating diffused fill from the front and sides; the moisture beads catch light sharply, suggesting a hard component within the otherwise controlled lighting setup; no atmospheric haze is present, but surface condensation creates a tactile, cold visual cue. Subject Geometry & Materiality: Each subject is a tall, cylindrical aluminum can with smooth vertical walls and rounded rims; both are coated in matte white printed labels with bold, high-contrast typography; circular color graphics are printed flat onto the surface—{argument name="left can color" default="magenta and red"} on the left can, {argument name="right can color" default="yellow and green"} on the right can; the aluminum surfaces are covered with uniformly distributed water droplets of varying diameters, clinging via surface tension; droplets create micro-lens effects, distorting underlying text and graphics; edges are crisp, with no deformation, indicating rigid packaging. Environmental Layering: The foreground consists of a horizontal metallic ledge with linear grooves and visible fasteners, rendered in sharp focus; the cans sit directly atop this ledge, establishing physical contact; the midground is entirely occupied by the cans; the background is a uniform, out-of-focus deep red gradient wall with subtle tonal variation and no discernible texture; no additional objects or layers are present beyond these three planes. Technical Artifacts & Color: The color palette contrasts cool whites and saturated accent colors on the cans against a warm, dark red background; saturation is moderate to high in the printed circles, while the background remains subdued; fine film grain is visible across the image, especially in the darker red areas, suggesting either high ISO or intentional texture; slight vignetting darkens the frame edges; no chromatic aberration or motion blur is visible; highlights on droplets are sharp with controlled roll-off. TEXT: Title: “IMAGE & COMMERCE”; Subtitle: “Cinematic prompt just for you” (partially visible); Body: Flavor names including “{argument name="left flavor" default="Raspberry Guava"}” on the left can and “Lemon Lime” on the right can; CTA: None; Logo: “I&C”; Disclaime
```

![四角电影面板构图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100869469_n0tslw_HALVLKkbMAAnKr3.jpg)
![四角电影面板构图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100870972_1wvoet_HALVK97aAAAQhRT.jpg)

```
Create a single cinematic image divided into four horizontal panels, each panel representing a different camera angle of the same scene and subject.
All panels must be visually cohesive in lighting, color grading, and atmosphere.
Top panel – BIRD’S-EYE SHOT:
A top-down overhead view, perfectly vertical camera angle, emphasizing spatial layout and geometry.
Second panel – SIDE CLOSE-UP SHOT:
A close-up shot from the side profile, shallow depth of field, focusing on facial or object details with cinematic compression.
Third panel – EXTREME CLOSE-UP:
An extreme close-up capturing fine textures and micro details, filling the frame almost abstractly.
Bottom panel – MEDIUM WIDE BACK SHOT:
A medium-wide shot from behind the subject, showing posture and environment, cinematic framing, strong sense of depth.
Clean horizontal separations between panels, editorial film-strip composition, high-end cinematic still, consistent subject identity across all panels.
```

### 200. 在 Nano Banana Pro 中控制事件时序的提示

**Author**: [توليف](https://x.com/tawleefai)  **Date**: 2026-02-02  **Language**: en

> 用户提供了一个特定的短语，用于 Nano Banana Pro 的提示词中，以控制生成图像中事件的时间，从而允许用户请求在主场景“之前”或“之后”发生的事情。

![在 Nano Banana Pro 中控制事件时序的提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100853376_pfc13o_HALHajTW8AAC5Ts.jpg)

```
Show me what occurs before/After.
أرني ما يحدث قبل/بعد ذلك.
```
